3 import scala.concurrent._
4 import javax.inject._
5 import play.api._
6 import play.api.db.slick.{DatabaseConfigProvider, HasDatabaseConfigProvider}
7 import play.api.libs.json._
8 import play.api.mvc._
9 import slick.jdbc.JdbcProfile
10 import slick.jdbc.PostgresProfile.api._

12 import whatson.db.EventTable._
13 import whatson.db.Util._
14 import whatson.model._
15 import whatson.model.Event._

17 import com.mohiva.play.silhouette.api._

25 /**
26  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
27  */
28 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
29                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
30                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
31                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
32                                 val userService: UserService,
33                                 eventService: EventService,
34                                 locationService: LocationService,
35                                 importService: ImportService)
36     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
37     extends AbstractController(cc)
38     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
39     with Util {
40 
41   val log = Logger("api.event")
42 
43   def getEvent(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
44     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
45 
46     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
47 
48     db.run(q.detailed).map(x => x.headOption match {
49       case Some(r) => Ok(Json.toJson(r))
50       case _ => NotFound
51     })
52   }
53 
54   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Int], category: Option[Int],
55                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
56     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
57     
58     val q = for {
59       e <- event if e.name like search.map(y => "%"++y++"%").getOrElse("%%").bind
60                  /*if similar(e.name,search.getOrElse("").bind) || search.getOrElse("").bind === ""*/
61                  if e.categories.filter(_.id === category.getOrElse(-1)).exists || category.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
62                  if e.locationId - location.getOrElse(-1).bind === 0 || location.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
63                  if e.from >= from.getOrElse(new Timestamp(0,0,0,0,0,0,0)) && e.from <= to.getOrElse(new Timestamp(4000,0,0,0,0,0,0))
64                  if e.to.getOrElse(plus(e.from,oneDay)) >= currentTimestamp
65     } yield e
66 
67 
68 
69     val s = q.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
70     returnPaged(s,q,db)
71   }
72 
73   def getNearby(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
74     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
75 
76     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
77 
78     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
79       case Some(e) => {
80         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
81           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, e.location.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, 
82               y._2.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f), y._2.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f)))
83           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
84         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
85         returnPaged(s,q,db)
86       }
87       case None => Future(NotFound)
88     }
89   }
90 
91   def getSameViewed(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
92     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
93 
94     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
95       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
96       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
97       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
98 
99     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
100 
101     returnPaged(s,q,db)
102   }
103 
104   def deleteEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
105     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
106 
107     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
108 
109     db.run(q).map {
110       case 0 => NotFound
111       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
112     }
113   }
114 
115   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
116     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
117       form => {
118         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
119       },
120       data => {
121         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
122 
123         eventService.insertEvent(data, organizer).map {
124           case Some(ev) => Ok(Json.toJson(ev))
125           case None => BadRequest
126         }
127       })
128   }
129 
130   def updateEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
131     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
132       form => {
133         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
134       },
135       data => {
136         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
137 
138         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
139 
140         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
141 
142         val catParents = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
143             case cat =>
144               cat.id match {
145                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).flatMap(_.parent).result
146               }
147           }
148 
149         val catSimple = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
150             case cat =>
151               cat.id match {
152                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
153               }
154           }
155         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(catSimple ++ catParents).map(_.flatten.distinct)
156 
157         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
158 
159         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
160           case (((images,categories),Some(event)),Some(location)) => {
161             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to,
162                               data.description,
163                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
164                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
165 
166             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
167 
168             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
169               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
170           }
171           case _ => Future.successful(None)
172         }.flatMap {
173           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
174             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
175             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
176             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
177 
178             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event, img._2))
179             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
180             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
181             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
182           }
183           case None => Future.successful(None)
184         }.map {
185           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
186           case None => BadRequest
187         }
188       })
189   }
190 
191   def insertCSV = organizerRequest(parse.multipartFormData) { case (request,organizer) =>
192     log.debug("Rest request to insert events by csv")
193 
194     request.body.file("csv").map { case x =>
195       val file = x.ref.path.toFile()
196 
197       eventService.insertCSV(file,organizer)
198      }.map(_.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))).headOption.getOrElse(Future.successful(BadRequest))
199   }
200 
201   def participate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
202     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
203 
204     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
205       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).result)
206 
207     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
208       case (Some(e),None) => {
209         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1),id)))
210         Future.successful(Ok)
211       }
212       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
213       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
214     }
215   }
216 
217   def unparticipate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
218     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
219 
220     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).delete)
221       .flatMap {
222       case 1 => {
223         Future.successful(Ok)
224       }
225       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
226     }
227   }
228 
229   def getSliderEvents = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
230     log.debug("Rest request to get events for slider")
231 
232     db.run(SliderEventTable.sliderEvent.sortBy(_.number).flatMap(_.event).detailed).map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))
233   }
234 
235   def importFacebookEvent(url: String) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
236     log.debug("Rest request to import event from url")
237 
238     importService.getEvent(url, request.identity)
239       .map(x => x.map(y => Ok(Json.toJson(y))).getOrElse(BadRequest))
240   }
241   
242   def copy(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
243     log.debug("Rest request to copy event")
244 
245     db.run(EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id && x.creatorId === organizer.id).detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
246       case Some(ev) => {
247         val locationForm = LocationForm.Data(ev.location.id, ev.location.name, ev.location.country,
248                                              ev.location.city, ev.location.street, ev.location.website,
249                                              ev.location.phone, ev.location.comment, ev.location.link, ev.location.zip)
250         val eventForm = EventForm.Data(ev.name, ev.from, ev.to, ev.categories.map(_.category), locationForm, 
251                                   ev.images.map(x => TaggedImageForm.Data(x.id.get, x.tag)), ev.description, ev.priceMin, ev.priceMax)
252         
253         eventService.insertEvent(eventForm, organizer).map {
254           case Some(event) => Ok(Json.toJson(event))
255           case _ => BadRequest
256         }
257       }
258       case None => Future.successful(BadRequest)
259     }
260   }
